Open Schools In Ontario For In Person Learning Immediately

Opening Schools & Daycares Full Time Safely In Ontario

In honour of Bell Let‚Äôs Talk Day on January 28‚Äô 2021 parents will be pulling their children out of virtual school to spread awareness, contact the media and hold a drive by rally Queens Park to be loud that mental health is being ignored and damaging our children‚Äôs and parents mental health. Mental health is being ignored. Decorate your car with signs to attract attention to spread awareness and walk safely outside holding signs if you can‚Äôt make it downtown.

We are a union of parents rallying to stand up for our children‚Äôs right to have in person learning resume immediately.

Schools and daycares should always be considered essential services. Remote learning does not work for many families and you have taken away our children‚Äôs rights to attend in person.
Closing schools and daycares for an extended period of time deeply affects our children‚Äôs mental health, education and safety. Schools are much safer than allowing families extra weeks off to break rules and not abide by guidelines which opens risk for more spread of the virus.

This decision to switch to online learning is also damaging our careers as parents financially and leaving an intense impact on our mental health. Many parents cannot stop working or afford childcare outside of school. Some families can‚Äôt afford to put food on the table and school is the only source for a child to eat daily. Parents like myself who are essential workers cannot be home with our children guiding them through remote learning daily. Many single parents living on one source of income cannot financially survive with remote learning and it will damage their sole source of income. This decision for remote learning has also pushed many families who can afford childcare to hire caregivers outside of their homes which is opening doors for more spread when our children could be attending school safely with their consistent cohort.

Not all children are safe at home. Children suffering from abuse within their home are not safe and school is often their only outlet for safety away from the daily child abuse. I speak for all children who are suffering from child abuse who have no voice due to fear of speaking out publicly and ask you to please always remember that school is imperative for education but also safety from child abuse.

Areas in the community that have been badly hit with covid need constant financial assistance, expanding testing, implementing a ban of evictions and paid sick leave for parents who cannot afford to stop working.
Why has there been such a delay in supporting these areas with high community spread? This should of been addressed and investigated much earlier to be prepared to act earlier.

We know you were under tremendous unnecessary pressures from boards to approve an extended holiday but we are still appalled you chose to cave. The spread of the virus is not happening within schools and being brought in from the community.

Y
YumNaturals Emporium Amandha Vollmer 19.01.2021 21:23:38
Vaccinated are at higher risk of flu AND all illness:

A 2011 study found that seasonal flu shots increase the risk of flu by 73% and doubled the risk of non-flu respiratory infections.

https://doi.org/10.1097/inf.0b013e318201811c

A 2011 study confirmed that annual influenza vaccination indeed hampers the development of a robust cell-mediated immunity. Annual vaccination for influenza, ‚Äúmay render young children who have not previously been infected with an influenza virus more susceptible to infection with a pandemic influenza virus of a novel subtype.‚Äù

https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC3209321/

A 2018 study found there was an increase of acute respiratory infections caused by non-influenza respiratory pathogens following influenza vaccination compared to unvaccinated children.

https://www.sciencedirect.com/science/article/pii/S0264410X18303153?via%3Dihub

Children who get the flu vaccine have 3x the risk of being hospitalized for flu.

https://www.sciencedaily.com/releases/2009/05/090519172045.htm

A 2014 study found that the more the people had been vaccinated in prior years, the less effective the vaccine is at preventing the most recent season‚Äôs dominant H3N2 virus.

As they put it, ‚Äúvaccine-induced protection was greatest for individuals not vaccinated during the prior 5 years.‚Äù

https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/25270645

Not only are there serious questions about the efficacy of the flu vaccine, there is evidence to suggest that getting the vaccine every year may cause damage to the immune system.

In a 2016 study, researchers found that people who were vaccinated against the flu three years in a row were actually at higher risk of being infected with the flu.

https://academic.oup.com/cid/article/63/1/21/1745238

Increased Risk of Noninfluenza Respiratory Virus Infections Associated With Receipt of Inactivated Influenza Vaccine

https://academic.oup.com/cid/article/54/12/1778/455098?searchresult=1

A randomized controlled trial in 2012 found that influenza-vaccinated children had no significantly lessened risk from influenza and also a higher risk of infection from non-influenza viruses.

https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC3404712/

Influenza virus made stronger by vaccines:

http://www.burnettcountysentinel.com/news/influenza-potentially-made-stronger-by-vaccines/article_4bd056da-0c21-11e8-b6ae-533d3d165845.html

Flu vaccine increases risk of upper respiratory infection:

https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/m/pubmed/22423139/

Flu vaccine makes people >6x more infectious than non-vaccinated when they contract influenza A:

http://www.pnas.org/content/early/2018/01/17/1716561115

2014 study - Influenza-like illness was more common in children vaccinated against influenza

https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/?term=24483149

https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/?term=29348203

A study that compared children who received the flu vaccine to those who did not found the same rate of influenza in both groups following vaccination. It also found that the group of children who received the flu vaccine had a 4.4 times higher rate of non-influenza respiratory tract infections.

https://academic.oup.com/cid/article/54/12/1778/455098

Annual influenza vaccination hampers the development of virus-specific CD8(+) T cell responses
https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/21880755/

Vaccination may make flu worse if exposed to a second strain

https://m.medicalxpress.com/news/2013-08-vaccination-flu-worse-exposed-strain.html

A review in the medical journal The Lancet found a lack of health benefits from influenza vaccine in children under two along with significantly increased rates of vaccine-related adverse events.

https://www.sciencedirect.com/science/article/abs/pii/S0140673605179847

A study published in Pediatrics International of Japanese children ages 6 months to 2 years who were vaccinated against the flu found that the influenza vaccine did not reduce the rate of influenza A infections in children under two.

https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/15056235/
